New loudness compensation effect will restore the brightness of the music played at the lowest volume levels.\r\n\r\nOther player features:\r\n- Can play .flac (on Windows 10) .mp3 .m4a/.m4b/.mp4/.aac .wav .wma .ac3 .3gp .3g2 .amr\r\n- Background playback and standard controls on lock screen\r\n- Next track selection: tap track and player will open it next\r\n- Covers and images gallery\r\n- Low power consumption\r\n- Playback schedule\r\n- Supports huge playlists\r\nOn Windows 10 with Anniversary Update:\r\n- Equalizer with 12 + 1 bands with Bark scale, 500 headphone presets and imitation profiles, loudness equalization in range from 20 to 80 Phon\r\n- Tube sound effect with six tube models\r\n- Noise gate effect\r\n- Gapless playback\r\n- Resampler\r\n\r\nCollection support:\r\n- Playlists automatically created from folders\r\n- Playlist editor with custom file picker\r\n- Quick add tracks to playlist or remove them using + and - buttons\r\n- Cover art downloader; if there is no image in folder of current track it will be found and downloaded from network within several seconds\r\n- Search by all tags at once: if you are looking for some rock from 70-s, just enter «Rock 197» in search box\r\n- Playlist tiles\r\n\r\nConverter (versions before Anniversary Update):\r\n- Can sort files by artist and album folders\r\n- Tube sound effect\r\n- Gaps reduction\r\n- Noise removal tool\r\n- Eight bands equalizer\r\n\r\nQuestions you may have\r\n\r\nQ: Tube sound on digital device? Is it possible?\r\nA: It is just math, player emulates single-ended triode amplifier. Some popular players on PC had similar plugins.\r\n\r\nQ: I do not see my music, where is it?\r\nA: If you do not see your music, please check that: \r\n1) On PC visit Settings > Collection > Folders and add custom music folders\r\n2) SD card is inserted and contacts are reliable.\r\n3) Check phone settings, check whether other apps can access files on SD card.\r\n4) Is there message that card has errors when phone is connected to PC with USB cable? If you have Card Reader on your PC or notebook, you may also try insert card and check it for errors.\r\n5) On smartphone files are copied to Music folder. By security reasons player can access only folder with name Music.\r\n6) Check file extensions. By example FLAC is supported only on Windows 10.
